the matrix by which if you multiply another matrix you get the same one back, it acts
like the number 1 ^jA4KsGBE

describe the sequence as a function of n ^Pk9m32Kv

sequence where each number is obtained by multiplying for a constant the previous
or by multiplying n times for a ratio ^oO1XmdjY

reverse the immaginary part, horizontal reflection on the complex plane ^LLAPfj1y

the angle in the complex plane, anticlockwise with the positive x axes ^kuBBR4v4
